<Text>I have been coming here for at least 30 years using the 100 yard rifle range most of the time but I have also used the pistol and archery ranges. The price is great and I've never had a bad experience here.

The rules need to be strict at any rifle range and they handle things here professionally and in a friendly manner. I've never had any range master constantly looking over my shoulder as some other reviewers have suggested.

I come here occasionally and I have no relationship with anyone in particular. I guess if you handle your range time in a proper manner with appropriate range etiquette you will not be harassed. If you make mistakes and do not understand the common safety rules of any range you can expect to be watched and you may have intervention from range staff for your own safety and the safety off others.

I've always enjoyed using the Manteca Sportsmen Inc. Range !!< /Text>< GmapID>

<response>None</response>< Text>
This range is questionable at best. The range masters have the worst professionalism I have ever seen at any range. They have zero patience for anybody and they will jump on you for anything minor infraction. Yes the prices are affordable but its not worth the experience. The place is run down and the 100 yard range make no sense at all. You have 3 spaces for rimfire only and the rest for center fire. A one shot per five second rule or they will bust you for rapid firing. The last time that I was there my father inquired about shooting our AR-15's at the 50 yard rimfire to see if it was ok. The gentleman at the office said it was perfectly fine for use to shoot at the 50 yard range. When we got over there, the range master immediately questioned us of why we were shooting and AR-15 on the rimfire only range. We replied that the gentleman in the office said it was fine for us to do so. He questioned us and told us that wasn't policy  , he also did this to another gentleman at the range. This lack of communication between the range and the office lead to a bad experience. What's sad it that this has been going on for the last few years. If this range wants to be able to compete with the other ranges around them, they should strongly consider friendlier staff members.</Text>

<review>In short: Friendly, honest, fast--in and out in less than 30 mins, cheap, and a great experience. I recommend this place to everyone.

At length:At first I walked in and I couldn't find anyone, the place looks like it's falling apart, and I wasn't sure what to think... Then I talked to Eddie and he was super friendly, and told me he'd be done with the guy in front of me in a few minutes. I was talking to the guy who's car he was working on, and he had an old Mercedes that "failed a bunch of smog tests" and he said that "the other place wanted to charge me 300$ to fix it". < Review>
I am sort of biased about Athena Grill. I have been going here for at least 15 years and have seen many changes. The Athena Grill today is putting out food almost like the first time I ate here.

Outside dining is available at this time but because of the red/orange tier levels, there is in door dining.

The food can be fantastic to good. Every place has a bad day but for the most part the food is very good. I enjoy the sample plate when I can't decide and the wife seems to order the gyro plate at every opportunity.

Service used to be great, now just slightly above average.

Still a most try for greek cuisine.< /Review>

<username>Eneru Montevedra</username><Date>1609053011733< /Date><rating>5<//rating>< review>
Right before my predecessor retired she said this restaurant is one of the Company favorites. To find a restaurant where everyone enjoys the food with no complaints is no small feat with this office.

Taki the Catering Director is awesome and always responds to my (multiple) questions and changes quickly. The Tri Tip (Moschari Psito) is amazing. Both of the chicken dishes that I have ordered (Chicken Souvlaki and Reganati) are phenomenal. All meats are always cooked perfectly, even with ordering for nearly 100. Everything is cooked perfectly including the rice and grilled vegetables. They don't skimp on the portions either. Thank you all so much!<//review>

Despite the pandemic, we had a really nice Monday afternoon lunch. Great service; fresh, delicious food; and well-spaced seating on the lovely patio. Construction noise across the street mostly faded into the background.

First visit after seeing this place reviewed on "Check, Please! Bay Area" and the show's unanimous positive reviews were spot on.

Decided to have a weekday lunch, went early, around 11:20a to beat the peak lunch crowd. The ordering line gets long very quickly around 11:45a and available table seating sparse soon thereafter.

My wife ordered the "Swordfish Souvlaki Wrap" and I the "Lamb Souvlaki Plate." The swordfish wrap was a bit messy to eat by hand with the fish and sauce juices dripping. The fish was seasoned well, not overly salted. Overall, delicious. The lamb plate came with a Greek style salad, sauteed veggies, decent portion side of rice, single kabob of well seasoned lamb. Again, tasty and enjoyable.

We plan to revisit and try other dishes.<//review>

The owner is so friendly. It's a great spot for lunch and dinner. The food is tasty, reasonably priced and they give you relatively large portions. Excellent food - biftekia, wraps, especially lamb pita wrap. You are not going to find lamb wraps/gyro in Greece now days, as the meat is too expensive vs what they can charge. Or you'll find it in the ground mix with more  herbs and fried oil then lamb. And all that  for 12$, in the heart of Silicon  Valley. Seems they make their own hummus and also, raspberry sauce you get with fries is awesome. Fries are extremely good. Seems they use good ingredients and know how to do it...

What's better than in Greece is the gyros comes with fries aside, not in the gyros.

The owner is always around and makes sure everything is right. Same employees for last 10 years tells a lot. Recently they've put lemons and olives around the place to make it look "right". Lots of outdoor seating< /review>

Excellent!  Came here for lunch with a friend for the first time. This place is no secret as evident by the big crowds. Downside is parking is tough. <review>Went to this place for the first time, yesterday, because my family saw them on Check Please Bay Area. We went here to celebrate a birthday and were hugely disappointed.

The visit was on Friday 8/14/18, at about 5:00pm . The place wasn't busy.

The food was average at best, but average is being nice.

The complementary meze hummus was the best item we ate. It tasted like it was made in house.

As for our meals.. I had the Gyros Plate. It had a generous amount of meat, tomato and red onion flooded with tzatziki sauce. A little restraint on the sauce would have been nicer. The meat was ok tasting andvedible. The side of Garlic fries had zero taste of garlic, was cold and limp and inedible.

Another member of my family had a plate with fish and shrimp of some kind and was also hugely disappointed. Way too much oil on the plate.

No server came to ask how everything  was, because we would have told them our fries were cold, limp, and didnt taste of garlic.

We couldn't get out of here soon enough.

< review>
We enjoyed the Greek food we had on a trip to Greece so we wanted to try this place since it had good ratings on Yelp.

It was disappointing.  Food was barely room temperature.  It was like taking out food from the fridge and letting the food sit out for a while to  make it room temperature.

We ordered chicken and beef souvlaki plate, mousaka, and octopus mezes.  We've had souvlaki and mousaka before so we know these are dishes are served hot (or at least warm).  We've never had mezes though so we're not even sure if that's supposed to be served with the octopus at least warm in a bed of greens, of it it just got cold.  The octopus was cooked tender though so one star for that.

The food looked really appetizing as we were watching the food taken out, but looks were deceiving.<//review>

Janet Fricke<//user_name>
<Date>1537834861472<//Date><Rating>2</Rating>< text>
I was excited to visit this eatery for seeing it on Check Please on PBS this weekend. While waiting in line to order (you order first, then find a table to sit)I saw delicious plates go buy. Unfortunately what I ordered was not freshly made. I had the combination platter. I was told they ran out of Pastitsio so I could substitute more Spanakopita or Mousaka or stuffed grape leaves. Unfortunately the Spanakopita and Moussaka were reheated, soggy and tasted rewarmed- not fresh. The french fries were also "limp and soggy" and "not crispy hot" and could not stand up to holding them to put into the small dish of delicious kalamata dipping  sauce. I expected the phyllo dough in the spanakopita to have a "crunch" but it was so soggy I had to cut it with a fork. what a disappointment. The Mousaka was not even thoroughly heated through and was dry. I think if I had selected a grilled skewer item cooked to order it would have been a better choice. My husband had the beef tenderloin skewer souvlaki. It was done perfectly to medium rare, juicy and hot.
The staff were very friendly and helpful.  I had told our server that I had just seen the restaurant on Check Please and so excited to come. She said it has been televised 3 times. Truly a disappointment for driving 40 miles one way.<//text>
